     1	import type {Codec} from './codec';
     2	import type {LogLevel} from './log-level';
     3	import {Log} from './logger';
     4	import {truthy} from './truthy';
     5	
     6	export const validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec = ({
     7	        width,
     8	        height,
     9	        codec,
    10	        scale,
    11	        wantsImageSequence,
    12	        indent,
    13	        logLevel,
    14	}: {
    15	        width: number;
    16	        height: number;
    17	        scale: number;
    18	        codec: Codec;
    19	        wantsImageSequence: boolean;
    20	        indent: boolean;
    21	        logLevel: LogLevel;
    22	}) => {
    23	        let actualWidth = width * scale;
    24	        let actualHeight = height * scale;
    25	        if (wantsImageSequence) {
    26	                return {
    27	                        actualWidth,
    28	                        actualHeight,
    29	                };
    30	        }
    31	
    32	        if (
    33	                codec !== 'h264-mkv' &&
    34	                codec !== 'h264' &&
    35	                codec !== 'h265' &&
    36	                codec !== 'h264-ts'
    37	        ) {
    38	                return {
    39	                        actualWidth,
    40	                        actualHeight,
    41	                };
    42	        }
    43	
    44	        if (
    45	                actualWidth % 1 !== 0 &&
    46	                (actualWidth % 1 < 0.005 || actualWidth % 1 > 0.005)
    47	        ) {
    48	                Log.verbose(
    49	                        {indent, logLevel},
    50	                        `Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${Math.round(actualWidth)}`,
    51	                );
    52	                actualWidth = Math.round(actualWidth);
    53	        }
    54	
    55	        if (
    56	                actualHeight % 1 !== 0 &&
    57	                (actualHeight % 1 < 0.005 || actualHeight % 1 > 0.005)
    58	        ) {
    59	                Log.verbose(
    60	                        {indent, logLevel},
    61	                        `Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${Math.round(actualHeight)}`,
    62	                );
    63	                actualHeight = Math.round(actualHeight);
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        const displayName = codec === 'h265' ? 'H265' : 'H264';
    67	
    68	        if (actualWidth % 2 !== 0) {
    69	                const message = [
    70	                        `Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a width of ${actualWidth}px, which is an uneven number.`,
    71	                        `The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two.`,
    72	                        scale === 1
    73	                                ? `Change the width to ${Math.floor(width - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
    74	                                : `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original width is ${width} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual width.`,
    75	                ]
    76	                        .filter(truthy)
    77	                        .join(' ');
    78	                throw new Error(message);
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        if (actualHeight % 2 !== 0) {
    82	                const message = [
    83	                        `Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a height of ${actualHeight}px, which is an uneven number.`,
    84	                        `The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two. `,
    85	                        scale === 1
    86	                                ? `Change the height to ${Math.floor(actualHeight - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
    87	                                : `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original height is ${height} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual height.`,
    88	                ].join(' ');
    89	                throw new Error(message);
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        return {
    93	                actualWidth,
    94	                actualHeight,
    95	        };
    96	};

"""Test script to reproduce the uneven dimensions issue with scale factors"""

# Simulate the current validation logic from validate-even-dimensions-with-codec.ts
def current_validate_logic(width, height, scale, codec):
    """Current implementation that throws errors for uneven dimensions"""
    actual_width = width * scale
    actual_height = height * scale
    
    # Simulate the rounding logic
    if actual_width % 1 != 0 and (actual_width % 1 < 0.005 or actual_width % 1 > 0.005):
        actual_width = round(actual_width)
        print(f"Rounded width to {actual_width}")
    
    if actual_height % 1 != 0 and (actual_height % 1 < 0.005 or actual_height % 1 > 0.005):
        actual_height = round(actual_height)
        print(f"Rounded height to {actual_height}")
    
    # Check for even dimensions (current logic that fails)
    if actual_width % 2 != 0:
        raise ValueError(f"Width {actual_width} is uneven for codec {codec}")
    
    if actual_height % 2 != 0:
        raise ValueError(f"Height {actual_height} is uneven for codec {codec}")
    
    return actual_width, actual_height

def proposed_validate_logic(width, height, scale, codec):
    """Proposed implementation that rounds down uneven dimensions"""
    actual_width = width * scale
    actual_height = height * scale
    
    # Round to nearest integer first
    actual_width = round(actual_width)
    actual_height = round(actual_height)
    
    # If still uneven, round down to nearest even number
    if actual_width % 2 != 0:
        actual_width = actual_width - 1
        print(f"Adjusted width from {actual_width + 1} to {actual_width} (even)")
    
    if actual_height % 2 != 0:
        actual_height = actual_height - 1
        print(f"Adjusted height from {actual_height + 1} to {actual_height} (even)")
    
    return actual_width, actual_height

def main():
    # Test case from PR description: 4000x2592 with scale factor 0.35
    width = 4000
    height = 2592
    scale = 0.35
    codec = "h264"
    
    print("=== Test Case from PR Description ===")
    print(f"Original dimensions: {width}x{height}")
    print(f"Scale factor: {scale}")
    
    # Calculate expected dimensions
    expected_width = width * scale
    expected_height = height * scale
    rounded_width = round(expected_width)
    rounded_height = round(expected_height)
    
    print(f"Expected scaled dimensions: {expected_width:.2f}x{expected_height:.2f}")
    print(f"Rounded dimensions: {rounded_width}x{rounded_height}")
    print(f"Are dimensions even? Width: {rounded_width % 2 == 0}, Height: {rounded_height % 2 == 0}")
    
    print("\n=== Current Logic (should fail) ===")
    try:
        result = current_validate_logic(width, height, scale, codec)
        print(f"Success: {result[0]}x{result[1]}")
    except ValueError as e:
        print(f"Error: {e}")
    
    print("\n=== Proposed Logic (should work) ===")
    try:
        result = proposed_validate_logic(width, height, scale, codec)
        print(f"Success: {result[0]}x{result[1]}")
    except ValueError as e:
        print(f"Error: {e}")
    
    # Test some edge cases
    print("\n=== Edge Cases ===")
    test_cases = [
        (1920, 1080, 0.5),  # Results in 960x540 (both even)
        (1921, 1081, 0.5),  # Results in 960.5x540.5 -> 960x540 (both even)
        (4001, 2593, 0.35), # Similar to PR case
        (100, 100, 0.33),   # Results in 33x33 (both uneven)
        (101, 101, 1.0),    # Uneven dimensions at scale 1
    ]
    
    for w, h, s in test_cases:
        print(f"\nTesting {w}x{h} with scale {s}:")
        try:
            result = proposed_validate_logic(w, h, s, codec)
            print(f"  Result: {result[0]}x{result[1]}")
        except ValueError as e:
            print(f"  Error: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()'

/** Proposed fixed logic */
function fixedValidationLogic(width, height, scale, codec) {
    let actualWidth = width * scale;
    let actualHeight = height * scale;
    
    // Simulate the relevant codec check 
    const relevantCodecs = ['"'"'h264-mkv'"'"', '"'"'h264'"'"', '"'"'h265'"'"', '"'"'h264-ts'"'"'];

    actualHeight = Math.round(actualHeight);

    }

str_replace_editor create /testbed/packages/renderer/src/test/validate-even-dimensions.test.ts --file_text 'import {describe, expect, test} from '"'"'bun:test'"'"';
import {validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec} from '"'"'../validate-even-dimensions-with-codec'"'"';

describe('"'"'validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec'"'"', () => {
	test('"'"'should handle the PR case - 4000x2592 with scale 0.35'"'"', () => {
		const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
			width: 4000,
			height: 2592,
			scale: 0.35,
			codec: '"'"'h264'"'"',
			wantsImageSequence: false,
			indent: false,
			logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"',
		});

		// Should adjust height from 907 (uneven) to 906 (even)
		expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(1400);
		expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(906);
		expect(result.actualWidth % 2).toBe(0);
		expect(result.actualHeight % 2).toBe(0);
	});

	test('"'"'should handle small uneven dimensions'"'"', () => {
		const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
			width: 100,
			height: 100,
			scale: 0.33,
			codec: '"'"'h264'"'"',
			wantsImageSequence: false,
			indent: false,
			logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"',
		});

		// 33x33 should become 32x32 (both even)
		expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(32);
		expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(32);
		expect(result.actualWidth % 2).toBe(0);
		expect(result.actualHeight % 2).toBe(0);
	});

	test('"'"'should handle large uneven dimensions'"'"', () => {
		const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
			width: 1921,
			height: 1081,
			scale: 0.5,
			codec: '"'"'h265'"'"',
			wantsImageSequence: false,
			indent: false,
			logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"',
		});

		// 960.5x540.5 should become 960x540 (both even)
		expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(960);
		expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(540);
		expect(result.actualWidth % 2).toBe(0);
		expect(result.actualHeight % 2).toBe(0);
	});

	test('"'"'should return even dimensions unchanged'"'"', () => {
		const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
			width: 1920,
			height: 1080,
			scale: 0.5,
			codec: '"'"'h264'"'"',
			wantsImageSequence: false,
			indent: false,
			logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"',
		});

		// 960x540 should remain unchanged (both even)
		expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(960);
		expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(540);
		expect(result.actualWidth % 2).toBe(0);
		expect(result.actualHeight % 2).toBe(0);
	});

	test('"'"'should return as-is for image sequences'"'"', () => {
		const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
			width: 1921,
			height: 1081,
			scale: 0.5,
			codec: '"'"'h264'"'"',
			wantsImageSequence: true,
			indent: false,
			logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"',
		});

		// Should return exact scaled values for image sequences
		expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(960.5);
		expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(540.5);
		// Dimensions might be uneven for image sequences
	});

	test('"'"'should return as-is for non-H.264 codecs'"'"', () => {
		const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
			width: 1921,
			height: 1081,
			scale: 0.5,
			codec: '"'"'prores'"'"',
			wantsImageSequence: false,
			indent: false,
			logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"',
		});

		// Should return exact scaled values for non-H.264 codecs
		expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(960.5);
		expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(540.5);
		// Dimensions might be uneven for non-H.264 codecs
	});

	test('"'"'should handle fractional scale non-H.264 codec'"'"', () => {
		const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
			width: 4000,
			height: 2592,
			scale: 0.35,
			codec: '"'"'vp8'"'"',
			wantsImageSequence: false,
			indent: false,
			logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"',
		});

		// Should return exact scaled values for VP8 codec
		expect(result.actualWidth).toBeCloseTo(1400);
		expect(result.actualHeight).toBeCloseTo(907.2);
	});

	test('"'"'should handle typical SD resolution with scale 1'"'"', () => {
		const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
			width: 640,
			height: 480,
			scale: 1,
			codec: '"'"'h264'"'"',
			wantsImageSequence: false,
			indent: false,
			logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"',
		});

		// Already even dimensions should remain unchanged
		expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(640);
		expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(480);
		expect(result.actualWidth % 2).toBe(0);
		expect(result.actualHeight % 2).toBe(0);
	});

	test('"'"'should handle uneven dimensions with scale 1'"'"', () => {
		const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
			width: 641,
			height: 481,
			scale: 1,
			codec: '"'"'h264'"'"',
			wantsImageSequence: false,
			indent: false,
			logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"',
		});

		// Uneven dimensions should be adjusted to even
		expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(640);
		expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(480);
		expect(result.actualWidth % 2).toBe(0);
		expect(result.actualHeight % 2).toBe(0);
	});
});'

const { validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec } = require('"'"'/testbed/packages/renderer/dist/validate-even-dimensions-with-codec.js'"'"');

console.log("=== Testing Edge Cases ===");

// Test rounding behavior with various decimal values
const edgeCases = [
    { width: 1001, height: 1001, scale: 0.1, description: "Both odd, small scale" }, // 100.1x100.1
    { width: 1002, height: 1002, scale: 0.1, description: "Both even, small scale" }, // 100.2x100.2
    { width: 1003, height: 1003, scale: 0.1, description: "Both odd, small scale" }, // 100.3x100.3
    { width: 1004, height: 1004, scale: 0.1, description: "Both even, small scale" }, // 100.4x100.4
    { width: 999, height: 999, scale: 0.67, description: "Odd dimensions, fractional scale" }, // ≈669.33
    { width: 1000, height: 1000, scale: 0.67, description: "Even dimensions, fractional scale" }, // 670
    { width: 1, height: 1, scale: 0.5, description: "Minimum dimensions, fractional scale" }, // 0.5 -> 0
    { width: 3, height: 3, scale: 0.5, description: "Small odd dimensions, fractional scale" }, // 1.5 -> 2 -> 2
    { width: 5, height: 5, scale: 0.4, description: "Small odd dimensions, fractional scale" }, // 2 -> 2
];

edgeCases.forEach(({ width, height, scale, description }) => {
    console.log(`\n${description}: ${width}x${height} with scale ${scale}`);
    
    // Test with H.264 codec (should adjust)
    const h264Result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
        width, height, scale, codec: '"'"'h264'"'"', 
        wantsImageSequence: false, indent: false, logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"'
    });
    
    console.log(`  H.264 result: ${h264Result.actualWidth}x${h264Result.actualHeight}`);
    console.log(`  Even dimensions? Width: ${h264Result.actualWidth % 2 === 0}, Height: ${h264Result.actualHeight % 2 === 0}`);
    
    // Test with VP8 codec (should not adjust)
    const vp8Result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
        width, height, scale, codec: '"'"'vp8'"'"', 
        wantsImageSequence: false, indent: false, logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"'
    });
    
    console.log(`  VP8 result: ${vp8Result.actualWidth}x${vp8Result.actualHeight}`);
});

// Test case where dimensions become zero after scaling
console.log("\n=== Testing Zero Dimensions Edge Case ===");
try {
    const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
        width: 1, height: 1, scale: 0.1, codec: '"'"'h264'"'"',
        wantsImageSequence: false, indent: false, logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"'
    });
    console.log(`Result: ${result.actualWidth}x${result.actualHeight}`);
    console.log("Note: Zero dimensions may be valid for some edge cases");
} catch (error) {
    console.log(`Error: ${error.message}`);
}

h264Variants.forEach(codec => {
    const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
        width: 1001, height: 1001, scale: 1, codec,
        wantsImageSequence: false, indent: false, logLevel: '"'"'info'"'"'
    });
    console.log(`${codec}: ${result.actualWidth}x${result.actualHeight}`);
});

// Test max safe integer edge case

});

+import {describe, expect, test} from 'bun:test';
+import {validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec} from '../validate-even-dimensions-with-codec';
+
+describe('validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec', () => {
+test('should handle the PR case - 4000x2592 with scale 0.35', () => {
+const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
+width: 4000,
+height: 2592,
+scale: 0.35,
+codec: 'h264',
+wantsImageSequence: false,
+indent: false,
+logLevel: 'info',
+});
+
+// Should adjust height from 907 (uneven) to 906 (even)
+expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(1400);
+expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(906);
+expect(result.actualWidth % 2).toBe(0);
+expect(result.actualHeight % 2).toBe(0);
+});
+
+test('should handle small uneven dimensions', () => {
+const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
+width: 100,
+height: 100,
+scale: 0.33,
+codec: 'h264',
+wantsImageSequence: false,
+indent: false,
+logLevel: 'info',
+});
+
+// 33x33 should become 32x32 (both even)
+expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(32);
+expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(32);
+expect(result.actualWidth % 2).toBe(0);
+expect(result.actualHeight % 2).toBe(0);
+});
+
+test('should handle large uneven dimensions', () => {
+const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
+width: 1921,
+height: 1081,
+scale: 0.5,
+codec: 'h265',
+wantsImageSequence: false,
+indent: false,
+logLevel: 'info',
+});
+
+// 960.5x540.5 should become 960x540 (both even)
+expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(960);
+expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(540);
+expect(result.actualWidth % 2).toBe(0);
+expect(result.actualHeight % 2).toBe(0);
+});
+
+test('should return even dimensions unchanged', () => {
+const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
+width: 1920,
+height: 1080,
+scale: 0.5,
+codec: 'h264',
+wantsImageSequence: false,
+indent: false,
+logLevel: 'info',
+});
+
+// 960x540 should remain unchanged (both even)
+expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(960);
+expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(540);
+expect(result.actualWidth % 2).toBe(0);
+expect(result.actualHeight % 2).toBe(0);
+});
+
+test('should return as-is for image sequences', () => {
+const result = validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec({
+width: 1921,
+height: 1081,
+scale: 0.5,
+codec: 'h264',
+wantsImageSequence: true,
+indent: false,
+logLevel: 'info',
+});
+
+// Should return exact scaled values for image sequences
+expect(result.actualWidth).toBe(960.5);
+expect(result.actualHeight).toBe(540.5);
+// Dimensions might be uneven for image sequences

+indent: false,
+logLevel: 'info',
+});

+// Test the fixed behavior of validate-even-dimensions-with-codec.ts
+
+/** Proposed fixed logic */
+function fixedValidationLogic(width, height, scale, codec) {
+    let actualWidth = width * scale;
+    let actualHeight = height * scale;
+    
+    // Simulate the relevant codec check 
+    const relevantCodecs = ['h264-mkv', 'h264', 'h265', 'h264-ts'];
+    if (!relevantCodecs.includes(codec)) {
+        return { actualWidth, actualHeight };
+    }
+    
+    // Always round to nearest integer first
+    actualWidth = Math.round(actualWidth);
+    actualHeight = Math.round(actualHeight);
+    
+    // Adjust dimensions to be even by rounding down if necessary
+    console.log(`Initial rounded dimensions: ${actualWidth}x${actualHeight}`);
+    
+    if (actualWidth % 2 !== 0) {
+        console.log(`Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${actualWidth - 1}`);
+        actualWidth = actualWidth - 1;
+    }
+    
+    if (actualHeight % 2 !== 0) {
+        console.log(`Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${actualHeight - 1}`);
+        actualHeight = actualHeight - 1;
+    }
+    
+    return { actualWidth, actualHeight };
+}
+
+// Test the PR case
+console.log("=== Testing PR case: 4000x2592 with scale 0.35 ===");
+const result = fixedValidationLogic(4000, 2592, 0.35, 'h264');
+console.log("Result:", result);
+console.log("Width even?", result.actualWidth % 2 === 0);
+console.log("Height even?", result.actualHeight % 2 === 0);
+
+// Test additional edge cases
+console.log("\n=== Testing edge cases ===");
+
+const testCases = [
+    { width: 4000, height: 2592, scale: 0.35, codec: 'h264', expected: 'Should adjust height from 907 to 906' },
+    { width: 100, height: 100, scale: 0.33, codec: 'h264', expected: 'Should adjust both from 33 to 32' },
+    { width: 1920, height: 1080, scale: 0.5, codec: 'h264', expected: 'Should stay 960x540 (both even)' },
+    { width: 1921, height: 1081, scale: 0.5, codec: 'h264', expected: 'Should round both to even' },
+    { width: 4000, height: 2592, scale: 1.0, codec: 'prores', expected: 'Should return as-is (not h264 codec)' },
+];
+
+testCases.forEach(({ width, height, scale, codec, expected }) => {
+    console.log(`\nTesting ${width}x${height} with scale ${scale}, codec ${codec}:`);
+    console.log("Expected:", expected);
+    const result = fixedValidationLogic(width, height, scale, codec);
+    console.log("Result:", result);
+    console.log("Even dimensions? Width:", result.actualWidth % 2 === 0, "Height:", result.actualHeight % 2 === 0);
+});

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Test script to reproduce the uneven dimensions issue with scale factors"""
+
+# Simulate the current validation logic from validate-even-dimensions-with-codec.ts
+def current_validate_logic(width, height, scale, codec):
+    """Current implementation that throws errors for uneven dimensions"""
+    actual_width = width * scale
+    actual_height = height * scale
+    
+    # Simulate the rounding logic
+    if actual_width % 1 != 0 and (actual_width % 1 < 0.005 or actual_width % 1 > 0.005):
+        actual_width = round(actual_width)
+        print(f"Rounded width to {actual_width}")
+    
+    if actual_height % 1 != 0 and (actual_height % 1 < 0.005 or actual_height % 1 > 0.005):
+        actual_height = round(actual_height)
+        print(f"Rounded height to {actual_height}")
+    
+    # Check for even dimensions (current logic that fails)
+    if actual_width % 2 != 0:
+        raise ValueError(f"Width {actual_width} is uneven for codec {codec}")
+    
+    if actual_height % 2 != 0:
+        raise ValueError(f"Height {actual_height} is uneven for codec {codec}")
+    
+    return actual_width, actual_height
+
+def proposed_validate_logic(width, height, scale, codec):
+    """Proposed implementation that rounds down uneven dimensions"""
+    actual_width = width * scale
+    actual_height = height * scale
+    
+    # Round to nearest integer first
+    actual_width = round(actual_width)
+    actual_height = round(actual_height)
+    
+    # If still uneven, round down to nearest even number
+    if actual_width % 2 != 0:
+        actual_width = actual_width - 1
+        print(f"Adjusted width from {actual_width + 1} to {actual_width} (even)")
+    
+    if actual_height % 2 != 0:
+        actual_height = actual_height - 1
+        print(f"Adjusted height from {actual_height + 1} to {actual_height} (even)")
+    
+    return actual_width, actual_height
+
+def main():
+    # Test case from PR description: 4000x2592 with scale factor 0.35
+    width = 4000
+    height = 2592
+    scale = 0.35
+    codec = "h264"
+    
+    print("=== Test Case from PR Description ===")
+    print(f"Original dimensions: {width}x{height}")
+    print(f"Scale factor: {scale}")
+    
+    # Calculate expected dimensions
+    expected_width = width * scale
+    expected_height = height * scale
+    rounded_width = round(expected_width)
+    rounded_height = round(expected_height)
+    
+    print(f"Expected scaled dimensions: {expected_width:.2f}x{expected_height:.2f}")
+    print(f"Rounded dimensions: {rounded_width}x{rounded_height}")
+    print(f"Are dimensions even? Width: {rounded_width % 2 == 0}, Height: {rounded_height % 2 == 0}")
+    
+    print("\n=== Current Logic (should fail) ===")
+    try:
+        result = current_validate_logic(width, height, scale, codec)
+        print(f"Success: {result[0]}x{result[1]}")
+    except ValueError as e:
+        print(f"Error: {e}")
+    
+    print("\n=== Proposed Logic (should work) ===")
+    try:
+        result = proposed_validate_logic(width, height, scale, codec)
+        print(f"Success: {result[0]}x{result[1]}")
+    except ValueError as e:
+        print(f"Error: {e}")
+    
+    # Test some edge cases
+    print("\n=== Edge Cases ===")
+    test_cases = [
+        (1920, 1080, 0.5),  # Results in 960x540 (both even)
+        (1921, 1081, 0.5),  # Results in 960.5x540.5 -> 960x540 (both even)
+        (4001, 2593, 0.35), # Similar to PR case
+        (100, 100, 0.33),   # Results in 33x33 (both uneven)
+        (101, 101, 1.0),    # Uneven dimensions at scale 1
+    ]
+    
+    for w, h, s in test_cases:
+        print(f"\nTesting {w}x{h} with scale {s}:")
+        try:
+            result = proposed_validate_logic(w, h, s, codec)
+            print(f"  Result: {result[0]}x{result[1]}")
+        except ValueError as e:
+            print(f"  Error: {e}")
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()
